<div id="review_927205746" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/927205746" />
    <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27276528-liz"><img alt="✰ Liz ✰ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451097545p2/27276528.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/927205746?book_show_action=true">May 03, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✰ Liz ✰ " href="/user/show/27276528-liz">✰ Liz ✰ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=best-couples">best-couples</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=alpha-male-love">alpha-male-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=high-steam-alert">high-steam-alert</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=must-read">must-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=dark-and-gritty">dark-and-gritty</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer927205746" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10058607095841889794">Every once in a while I will come across a book that really stays with me. I want to talk to my husband about it over dinner. I want to go back and re-read my favorite parts. I want to ponder over the highlighted text. Monster in His Eyes is just that type of a read for me. I know that people have categorized it as a dark romance but truly I see it as so much more than that. I found this read to be thrilling, psychological, romantic, sexy, tender, gritty, and definitely unforgettable. I will do </span>
  <span id="freeText10058607095841889794" style="display:none">Every once in a while I will come across a book that really stays with me. I want to talk to my husband about it over dinner. I want to go back and re-read my favorite parts. I want to ponder over the highlighted text. Monster in His Eyes is just that type of a read for me. I know that people have categorized it as a dark romance but truly I see it as so much more than that. I found this read to be thrilling, psychological, romantic, sexy, tender, gritty, and definitely unforgettable. I will do my best in this review to do it justice. But truly, if you are at all intrigued by this book don't wait....read it NOW!<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412128509i/11328875.jpg" width="375" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Karissa is a young college student at NYU. She has lived a very sheltered life. Her mother is unstable and has moved them around quite a bit. She doesn't know her father. Karissa has made a life for herself in New York and she loves her roommate. After one drunk night out in the club, she meets an older man. That moment changes her life forever.<br><br><b>"Vitale. His full name is Ignazio Vitale, although once, not so long ago, he urged me to call him Naz. And it was Naz who charmed me, who won me over and made me melt . It wasn't until later that I got to know the true Ignazio, and by the time I met Vitale, it was far too late to just walk away. If I ever even could've…" </b><br><br>Naz is a "business man". He is attractive, wealthy, intelligent, and happily sweeps Karissa under his wings. Naz has a dark past. On one hand we see him trying to stay away from Karissa on the other hand he just cannot seem to stay away from her.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412128920i/11328998.jpg" width="250" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Karissa is smart enough to know that things are not quite above board regarding Naz's job. These suspicions are confirmed when she meets Naz's boss (who she recognizes as a mob boss). Despite the questionable lifestyle Naz lives, Karissa cannot seem to get enough of him. She is so willing to give herself to him. <br><br><b>"He's a child with a brand new toy, and I just hope he doesn't break me as soon as I'm out of the package." </b><br><br>They spend time together. Talking, eating dinners, making love, and all of the amazing things that new couples do. When these two come together....it is HOT!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412128921i/11328999._SY540_.jpg" width="375" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"I barely even register that the light is on anymore. The man is a wrecking ball, pounding me, and I come to pieces almost instantly."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412128509i/11328876.jpg" width="375" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Naz takes Karissa with him to Las Vegas. We begin to see the darker side of Naz. He is struggling with the monster within. Naz has warned Karissa that he isn't a good man. He offers her an out. She doesn't take it.<br><br><b>"I'm telling you," he says, his voice strained. "I'm warning you . I'm not a good man, Karissa, and I never will be. So don't think you can fix me, or that I'll ever change, because I won't. I can't. You have to know, if this goes any further, if you ask me to stay, I'm not going to be able to let you walk away."</b><br><br>Karissa doesn't want him to walk away....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412128509i/11328877._SY540_.jpg" width="375" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>As story begins to build, the tension is unreal. Karissa's mom has run away, Naz is mysteriously working (always wearing gloves), and Karissa and Naz are getting very serious. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412128509i/11328878.jpg" width="375" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Suddenly everything is revealed and it is UNBELIEVABLE. (Maybe other readers have been able to figure things out but I was completely BLOWN AWAY!) Karissa comes to the realization of who Naz really is. How can she still love him? How can she hate him? What does she do?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412128509i/11328879._SY540_.jpg" width="375" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Overall, I found Monster in His Eyes to be a fantastic read. I enjoyed the tension, the descriptive writing, the big reveal (aka cliffhanger), the beauty in Naz and Karissa's relationship, and the pacing was spot on! I wouldn't hesitate to recommend this book. Just be prepared to jump right into book 2 because you won't be able to wait to find out what happens!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412128509i/11328880._SY540_.jpg" width="375" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="10058607095841889794" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText14883721140916285306" style="display:none"><b>✮✮4.5 Stars✮✮</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398953670i/9487327._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="378" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><i>Monster in His Eyes</i> is a fast-paced, sexy read, that had my heart racing. <div id="review_917126810" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Catarina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina"><img alt="Catarina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514808293p2/11538033.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

<span id="freeTextContainer13003034278014636824"><b> 4 (Hesitant) Stars. </b>	<br/><br/>Karissa is a 18 years old college student that falls in love with an older guy. Naz is sexy, smart, irresistible…. And dangerous. <br/>She knows he’s not a good man, but she still can’t get away.   <span id="freeText13003034278014636824" style="display:none"><b> 4 (Hesitant) Stars. </b>	<br><br>Karissa is a 18 years old college student that falls in love with an older guy. Naz is sexy, smart, irresistible…. And dangerous. <br>She knows he’s not a good man, but she still can’t get away. There’s something pulling them together. <br>But as their romance starts to grow, she realizes that maybe their lives are more entwined that she thought. And now she has already too far in, to get back. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399075595i/9504568._SX540_.jpg" width="370" height="370" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There’s one thing Karissa will soon realize, when you fall in love with a monster how ready will you be when he is unleashed?<br>And when secrets start to get revealed, who is the real monster?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388683472i/7901653.jpg" width="350" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 4 Stars. 3 for the book, 1 plus for the author, because she wrote “Sempre” that is one of my favorite books of all time. I don’t care that we shouldn’t rate based on how we feel about the author, but meh, is my review so deal with it! :P <br> <b>Storyline: </b> This is not your traditional romance. It’s dark, raw and sexy. Although I liked I didn’t particularly liked the development of their relationship. I know that Naz is supped to be a dominant-sexy-badass, but still, in a lot of moments it seemed like he was almost forcing her to be with him. <br> <b>Writing Style: </b> First person, female POV. Amazingly written, emotional and engaging. I started this book before going to bed and let’s just say: I went to work very cranky due to the lack of sleep. <br> <b>Character Development: </b> I don’t love the “dark hero” that much, but with some annoyances I ended up liking Naz. The surprise was Karissa. Yes, she is completely naïve, but she is not annoying and I liked her a lot. <br> <b>Steam: </b> Hot. <br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Cliffhanger. But not a real bad one, just one that will make you want the next book very badly.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer917309545" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2164974218874949660"><b>6 (THIS IS THE BEST BOOK!!!!!) STARS</b><br/><br/>Beware, when I love a book hard, I go all fan girl mode.<br/><br/><b>I LOVE MONSTER IN HIS EYES!!!!!</b><br/><br/><b>I LOVE NAZ!!!!</b><br/><br/><b>IT WAS SOOOOOOO GOOOODDDD</b><br/><br/>There’s a reason why Monster In His Eyes has high ratings, it’s because it’s WONDERFUL!!!!!<br/><br/><b>Summary</b><br/><br/>Karissa is your typical college freshman. She’s on scholarship and has to maintain an overall GPA of 3.5 to keep it. She’s taking a philosophy class and is struggling in it. When she loses her phone, she goes back to class and meets Naz.<br/><br/>Naz</span>
  <span id="freeText2164974218874949660" style="display:none"><b>6 (THIS IS THE BEST BOOK!!!!!) STARS</b><br><br>Beware, when I love a book hard, I go all fan girl mode.<br><br><b>I LOVE MONSTER IN HIS EYES!!!!!</b><br><br><b>I LOVE NAZ!!!!</b><br><br><b>IT WAS SOOOOOOO GOOOODDDD</b><br><br>There’s a reason why Monster In His Eyes has high ratings, it’s because it’s WONDERFUL!!!!!<br><br><b>Summary</b><br><br>Karissa is your typical college freshman. She’s on scholarship and has to maintain an overall GPA of 3.5 to keep it. She’s taking a philosophy class and is struggling in it. When she loses her phone, she goes back to class and meets Naz.<br><br>Naz is a big mystery. He’s older, sexy and doesn’t say much. He hands Karissa her phone and they part ways. Then LATER she meets him again at a club! From there they date. Karissa knows there’s something dark about Naz, but she kind of puts it in the back burner because she is trying to feel instead of think. <br><br><b>Naz is the Hero I crave to love and hate all the same time. He’s damaged, torn, dark and oh so sexy. LICK</b><br><br><b>Review</b><br><br>The two main things that made this book just worked for me were the characters. I love them. Karissa is an awesome girl. She isn’t a ditz, but she does have that damsel in distress quality I love. Who doesn’t love a Heroine that is struggling in college and needs to keep her scholarship because she is poor? Karissa has a crazy over protective mother and it’s so wacky, it’s just another layer to add to Karissa’s crazy child hood.<br><br>The main star is Naz. Let’s take a moment to swoon. He’s 36 and there’s an 18 year age difference between Kariss and him. Is it creepy? No. It’s freaking sexy as heck. I guess I’m tired of reading books where the Hero is 25, to have the history Naz has, he needed to be older. My favorite part is just reading all the layers that come with Naz. He, as I said, is a big ball of mystery. You are going to eat him up! <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>They both take passion, someone getting under your skin and consuming you. And I ate you alive sweetheart. You never had a chance.<i><b></b></i></i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>The steam and chemistry is off the charts. There are intense steamy scenes and it’s so different and unique. I LOVE IT! Naz is the alpha male you want in books. He takes charge and doesn’t beat round the bush. If he wants something, he goes for it and doesn’t accept No. Again…. I love him.<br><br>You need to know there’s a cliffy, but it’s okay, it won’t kill you. You must read this book. It’s my top book for the year and Naz is my top book boyfriend. <br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21956060.Monster_in_His_Eyes__Monster_in_His_Eyes___1_" title="Monster in His Eyes (Monster in His Eyes, #1) by J.M. Darhower" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1398071281s/21956060.jpg" alt="Monster in His Eyes (Monster in His Eyes, #1) by J.M. Darhower" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1497585368/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=1497585368&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20&amp;linkId=XGDFEVC3AZJU3ODP" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a></span>

<div id="review_916268067" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/916268067" />
    <a title="Vanessa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12059859-vanessa"><img alt="Vanessa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576765878p2/12059859.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/916268067?book_show_action=true">Apr 21, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vanessa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vanessa" href="/user/show/12059859-vanessa">Vanessa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">ANYONE THAT LOVES FORBIDDEN, TABOO, AND/OR MAFIA ROMANCES</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=alpha-assholes-i-love">alpha-assholes-i-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=forbidden-taboo">forbidden-taboo</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=age-gap">age-gap</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=tortured-heros">tortured-heros</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=my-top-book-boyfriends">my-top-book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=sexy-billionaires">sexy-billionaires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=super-steamy">super-steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=favorite-couples">favorite-couples</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=revenge-is-a-dish-best-served-cold">revenge-is-a-dish-best-served-cold</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=dark-and-twisted-reads">dark-and-twisted-reads</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer916268067" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16957358091210515727"><b>5 OH MY Vitale Stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s996.photobucket.com/user/Vanessa_RB-Babe/media/MonsterinhisEyesCasting_zps4c380599.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414431023i/11653482._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo MonsterinhisEyesCasting_zps4c380599.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I loved this book!! Going straight into the next one. I know this book had some lovers (like ME) and some critics. This is actually part of the reason that I held back on diving into this series for so long, but I am SOOO glad that I did. It was mentioned in a private room where taboo love stories were being recommended and, I took it as a sign! :) <br/><br/>OMG Naz!!!! Naz <u>IS</u> this story!! Officially one of my top book boyfriends now. I won't tell you what Naz does for a living bu</span>
  <span id="freeText16957358091210515727" style="display:none"><b>5 OH MY Vitale Stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s996.photobucket.com/user/Vanessa_RB-Babe/media/MonsterinhisEyesCasting_zps4c380599.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414431023i/11653482._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo MonsterinhisEyesCasting_zps4c380599.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I loved this book!! Going straight into the next one. I know this book had some lovers (like ME) and some critics. This is actually part of the reason that I held back on diving into this series for so long, but I am SOOO glad that I did. It was mentioned in a private room where taboo love stories were being recommended and, I took it as a sign! :) <br><br>OMG Naz!!!! Naz <u>IS</u> this story!! Officially one of my top book boyfriends now. I won't tell you what Naz does for a living but let's just say, he's not a good guy. He's not honorable and is unapologetic about it. He's ruthless, lethal, and pretty much, just don't fuck with him! He sold his soul to the devil a long, long time ago. But of course, he wasn't always like that. And Karissa reminds him of a time, of a part of life, that can be different..better. But he is conflicted as hell over it. <br><br><b>
  <i>"I'm telling you," he says, voice strained. "I'm warning you. I'm not a good man, Karissa, and I will never be. So don't think you can fix me, or that I'll ever change, because I won't. I can't. You have to know, if this goes any further, if you ask me to stay, I'm not going to be able to let you walk away." <br><br>"If you could read my mind..." He pauses, laughing darkly. "You'd be trembling." - Ignazio</i>
</b><br><br>I know that Karissa had her fair share of critics out there. I actually didn't think she was immature at all. I mean, she is every bit of eighteen and nineteen years old. She says air-headed things sometimes. She has also led an extremely sheltered life and is on her own for the first time, going to school at NYU. But she was not whiny AT ALL and didn't bring a bunch of BS OTT drama to the story. I don't know, maybe another time, another book, she might've bothered me. But in this book? There was so much else that I was blown away by, that she just didn't. In fact, she was actually pretty determined in her feelings, which I loved. That's all I need. She handled all of this far better than I would've at 18-19 years old! <br><br>And did I mention that Naz is twice her age? He runs circles around her. So yes, there is a bit of a taboo element here. His maturity brought out her lack of, but, this seemed kind of real to me. We should notice an 18-year age difference. <br><br>I wish I would've read this book before <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12368985.Consequences__Consequences___1_" title="Consequences (Consequences, #1) by Aleatha Romig" rel="nofollow noopener">Consequences</a> and the like, because, in my opinion, THIS is a good revenge book with a believable and way better motive than some of the others I have read!!! But don't get me wrong, this is NOT a Stockholm syndrome book, in any way. If anything, I would compare the underlying themes to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7734384.Lili_Saint_Germain" title="Lili Saint Germain" rel="nofollow noopener">Lili Saint Germain</a>'s Gypsy Brothers series... the themes, not the story. Trying to be vague here and not give a crap ton away. ;) <br><br><a href="http://s996.photobucket.com/user/Vanessa_RB-Babe/media/MIHETeaser_zps74c071e1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414511560i/11661468._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo MIHETeaser_zps74c071e1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> &lt;---- YEAH! Did I mention that Naz takes the term "hate fucking" to a whole new level?!?!? OMG! Panty melting, is ALL I gotta say!!!<br><br>I could see where some might have found the beginning a bit on the slow side, but I still enjoyed every bit of it. The stage was being set for all that was to go down later. <br><br>Twist after twist leading up to a big HOLY SHIT ending!! By about half way into the book, I kind of predicted a part of it, but, again, didn't find that as a weakness of the story. I don't think it made it predictable. I think the author wanted us to figure part of it out. However, there were still a few twists that slapped me in the face with shock that I did NOT see coming!!!<br><br><b>
  <i>"My Prince Charming turned out to be the villain of my fairy tale, and part of me thinks that's okay, because eventually, it'll all disappear, anyway."</i>
</b> <br><br>Gah, there are SOO many more quotes that I want to include but they are major spoilers, so you will just have to read the book to enjoy them! <br><br>Dark complex characters, suspenseful, taboo, sexy...and a book that is thought provoking. Excellent! This is the kind of book that I LOVE to read!!!!<br><br>This was my first read by J.M Darhower. Why? I don't know. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18338465.Sempre__Forever___1_" title="Sempre (Forever, #1) by J.M. Darhower" rel="nofollow noopener">Sempre</a> has been on my TBR for what seems like forever. Well, I just moved it WAY up!! Really can't wait to read much more from this author very soon!! </span>
  <a data-text-id="16957358091210515727" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_922612981" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/922612981" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6049062-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460575899p2/6049062.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=new-adult-dark-contemporary">new-adult-dark-contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=dark-reads">dark-reads</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer922612981" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15917956472600373949">Monster in His Eyes is the first book in this dark but sexy story. I enjoyed the storyline on the whole, even though there were times when I felt it dragged a bit. There is a lot of secrets and mystery surrounding the hero..but not only him, I do feel that Karissa; the heroine has something in her family life that she is unaware of. I am not going to lie, alot of it was somewhat predictable as the story went along; but I was still able to enjoy the read.<br/><br/>The sex between Ignazio Vitale and Karissa</span>
  <span id="freeText15917956472600373949" style="display:none">Monster in His Eyes is the first book in this dark but sexy story. I enjoyed the storyline on the whole, even though there were times when I felt it dragged a bit. There is a lot of secrets and mystery surrounding the hero..but not only him, I do feel that Karissa; the heroine has something in her family life that she is unaware of. I am not going to lie, alot of it was somewhat predictable as the story went along; but I was still able to enjoy the read.<br /><br />The sex between Ignazio Vitale and Karissa are very heated! "Naz" is very passionate when it comes to Karissa, and his attraction to her is all consuming. That monster of his is lurking just under his surface, and when he wants to come out and play...it is nothing short of primal and animalistic! I loved every minute of those encounters when the beast would come out and play! My biggest complaint in this book was the heroine. I am finding a huge struggle with liking a lot of the heroines in any of the books that I read. They are out there; but they are few and far between!In Karissa's case, she really annoys me..and quite honestly whenever she asks Naz; "Why Her?" I think to myself..Ya...WHY her?! She just doesn't have the "wow" factor that I look for in the heroine's that I love. She is very gullible and trusts waaay too easy!<br /><br />I do not want to get into the story line as I am always scared I will leave something slip! This was an enjoyable read for me on the whole, and I am going to dive in to the second book right away! My fingers are crossed that Karissa will redeem herself and that Kaz will find much more calmness for his soul!</span>

<div id="review_3507687383" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Carmen Reyna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/57010433-carmen-reyna"><img alt="Carmen Reyna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1586936901p2/57010433.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3507687383?book_show_action=true">Sep 07, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carmen Reyna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carmen Reyna" href="/user/show/57010433-carmen-reyna">Carmen Reyna</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57010433-carmen-reyna?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57010433-carmen-reyna?shelf=good-but-not-good-enough">good-but-not-good-enough</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3507687383" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3025666975921203796"><b>Let me start by saying that the prologue of the book is kind of misleading.</b> Karissa doesn’t hate this man and the story is not dark and ugly for the most part.<br/><br/><b>Karissa is a college freshman who meets a man who she really shouldn’t be with.</b> Mainly because he’s much older and because what he does for a living is a mystery. <b>But he treats her right and really, she didn’t have a chance, he’s just too perfect and good to her.</b> That is, until who he really is comes to light and everything changes for her</span>
  <span id="freeText3025666975921203796" style="display:none"><b>Let me start by saying that the prologue of the book is kind of misleading.</b> Karissa doesn’t hate this man and the story is not dark and ugly for the most part.<br /><br /><b>Karissa is a college freshman who meets a man who she really shouldn’t be with.</b> Mainly because he’s much older and because what he does for a living is a mystery. <b>But he treats her right and really, she didn’t have a chance, he’s just too perfect and good to her.</b> That is, until who he really is comes to light and everything changes for her. But maybe it’s too late, because she’s already in love with him.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I'm not a good man, Karissa, and I never will be. So don't think you can fix me, or that I'll ever change, because I won't. I can't”<br /><br />“I'm not a man who just gives up in the middle of something. If I go any further, if I don't walk away now, I won't be able to.”<br /><br />“I know I should let you go, should let you walk away from me right now, but I can't do it. I can't.”<br /><br />“I've lost enough, Karissa. I won't lose you, too.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br /><br /><b>The plot did have a lot of potential, and I don’t know if I had really high expectations or what was it, but it just didn’t do it for me.</b> I didn’t like this as much as I thought I would. I’m disappointed because I was really looking forward to this.<br /><br /><b>This book made me think of how stupid love can make you.</b> I mean, she basically said she loved him without knowing anything about him. It simply didn’t interest me enough. <b>It was good enough to finish it but not good enough to want to read it all the time or want to finish it in a couple of days.</b> In fact, it took me a while to finish reading it and it felt more like homework because I was already more than 50% in.<br /><br /><b>Karissa seemed a little immature for my taste.</b> Just going blindly with whatever Naz said and it bugged me a little. I guess it made sense with the way she was raised but I rolled my eyes more than once at the way she rationalized everything he said and did.<br /><br /><b>Final thoughts:</b> it wasn’t bad but it wasn’t good either😬 and I don’t know if I’m gonna be reading the second book in the series even though I’m dying to see how their relationship will develop.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>I once thought the reality couldn't be as fascinating as the fantasy, but I was wrong. So very wrong.<br /><br />My voice is weak when I whisper, <b>"You don't love me."<br />"Oh, but I do,"</b> he says. <b>"Because if I didn't? You'd be dead already.”</b></i>
</blockquote><br /></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ttnjS8ec27Sse9gTr1XPkk4WEkJ2C6T5+bcWrLL7oL7Ez19AMJrGCGJ7dtU8gmXl7ZFNFh5exvE3lioXPT65Eg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('GGGzwUy0ZngCM/E0MY3we1wiBM17CjxPclUkM3dNBzxqdw/Ku7J7xMwzX/KiWloM/6VbmRNfXke8dBiI+IgekA==')})
  }

Luca is the future Capo of the New York Famiglia, a man known for his brutality—and for crushing his cousin’s throat with his bare hands.\nAria is terrified of marrying a monster like him. He may be one of the most sought-after bachelors in New York, thanks to his good looks, wealth and predator-like charisma. But Aria knows the bad boy aura isn’t just a game; blood and death lurk beneath Luca’s striking gray eyes and arrogant smile.\nIn her world a handsome exterior often hides the monster within; a monster who can just as easily kill as kiss you.\nYet, there’s no escaping the arranged bond, much less a man like Luca. He’d follow her to the end of the world.\nHer only chance to survive in a marriage with Luca is to gain his affection and work her way into his heart—even when rumor has it that Luca doesn’t have a
